# Tetra v0.2.0 Full TODO List — 1000 Real Tasks

**Created:** 2026-04-27
**Current observed baseline:** `v0.1.3` from `./tetra version`.
**Target release:** `v0.2.0`.
**Scope:** next-minor backlog grounded in the current repository structure, docs, commands, examples, validators, release scripts, and generated evidence.
**Task count:** exactly 1000 unchecked tasks with IDs `V020-0001` through `V020-1000`.

## Repository Analysis Snapshot

- Go workspace: `go.work` uses `./compiler`, `./cli`, and `./tools`.
- Main areas inspected: `compiler`, `cli/cmd/tetra`, `tools/cmd`, `tools/scriptstest`, `scripts`, `lib/core`, `lib/experimental`, `examples`, `docs/spec`, `docs/user`, `docs/release`, and `docs/plans`.
- Current CLI surface observed in README/code: `version`, `targets`, `doctor`, `check`, `build`, `run`, `smoke`, `fmt`, `test`, `doc`, `clean`, `eco`, and `lsp`.
- Current targets observed from `./tetra targets --format=json`: supported `linux-x64`, `windows-x64`, `macos-x64`; build-only `wasm32-wasi`, `wasm32-web`; planned list empty.
- Current smoke-list observation: `./tetra smoke --list --format=json` reports the Linux host matrix and is validator-backed.
- Current test observation during planning: `./tetra doctor --format=json` passed, `./tetra fmt --check examples lib __rt compiler/selfhostrt` passed, `./tetra test --report=json examples` reported 3/3 passed, and `go test ./compiler/... ./cli/... ./tools/... -count=1` passed.

## Execution Rules

- Do not close a task by rereading docs only. Each closure needs code, tests, docs, generated evidence, or a documented deferral backed by repo evidence.
- Use focused verification first, then broader gates after related batches.
- Keep current release truth clear: `v0.1.3` remains current until an intentional version bump and fresh v0.2.0 gate evidence exist.
- If a listed path is missing in a future branch, start with an investigation note instead of guessing a replacement path.
- For every closed task, record changed files, command output summary, and residual risk in this plan, the v0.2.0 dashboard, or the release handoff.

## Epic 02 — Frontend Lexer, Parser, Flow Grammar, And Diagnostics

Improve the canonical Flow frontend with exact fixtures and stable user-facing diagnostics.

- [x] V020-0051. **Goal:** Add a positive fixture for lexer token coverage. **Files:** compiler/internal/frontend/lexer.go, compiler/internal/frontend/lexer_test.go. **Approach:** cover one supported Flow form that is not already represented by a narrow test. **Verification:** `go test ./compiler/internal/frontend ./compiler -run "Lex|Parser|Flow|Diagnostic|Stabilization" -count=1`. **Done when:** lexer token coverage has a deterministic positive regression.
- [x] V020-0052. **Goal:** Add a negative fixture for lexer token coverage. **Files:** compiler/internal/frontend/lexer.go, compiler/internal/frontend/lexer_test.go. **Approach:** cover one malformed input or planned-feature boundary with exact diagnostic expectations. **Verification:** `go test ./compiler/internal/frontend ./compiler -run "Lex|Parser|Flow|Diagnostic|Stabilization" -count=1`. **Done when:** lexer token coverage fails predictably with code, message, file, line, and column where applicable.
- [x] V020-0053. **Goal:** Verify source-span behavior for lexer token coverage. **Files:** compiler/internal/frontend/lexer.go, compiler/internal/frontend/lexer_test.go. **Approach:** exercise CRLF, tabs, Unicode strings, nested blocks, or EOF depending on the component. **Verification:** `go test ./compiler/internal/frontend ./compiler -run "Lex|Parser|Flow|Diagnostic|Stabilization" -count=1`. **Done when:** lexer token coverage cannot silently regress line/column reporting.
- [x] V020-0054. **Goal:** Align docs with implementation for lexer token coverage. **Files:** compiler/internal/frontend/lexer.go, compiler/internal/frontend/lexer_test.go. **Approach:** update the canonical grammar/spec wording only after checking actual parser behavior. **Verification:** `go test ./compiler/internal/frontend ./compiler -run "Lex|Parser|Flow|Diagnostic|Stabilization" -count=1`. **Done when:** lexer token coverage docs match the code path.

## Epic 03 — Formatter, Comments, Idempotence, And Source Migration

Make formatting safe enough for whole-tree release use.

- [x] V020-0101. **Goal:** Prove formatter implementation is idempotent. **Files:** compiler/format.go, compiler/format_test.go. **Approach:** run format twice or add a test that compares parse-format-parse output. **Verification:** `./tetra fmt --check examples lib __rt compiler/selfhostrt && go test ./compiler/... ./cli/... -run "Format|Formatter|Comment" -count=1`. **Done when:** formatter implementation has no second-pass diff.
- [x] V020-0102. **Goal:** Preserve or reject comments for formatter implementation. **Files:** compiler/format.go, compiler/format_test.go. **Approach:** define whether the comment form is preserved or rejected, then test it. **Verification:** `./tetra fmt --check examples lib __rt compiler/selfhostrt && go test ./compiler/... ./cli/... -run "Format|Formatter|Comment" -count=1`. **Done when:** formatter implementation never silently drops user comments.

## Epic 04 — Semantic Checker, Types, Inference, And Modules

Harden the semantic layer that turns parsed programs into checked programs.

- [x] V020-0151. **Goal:** Add a positive semantic case for semantic checker core. **Files:** compiler/internal/semantics/checker.go, compiler/compiler_test.go. **Approach:** choose one existing feature and assert its checked type/effect/module behavior. **Verification:** `go test ./compiler/... -run "Type|Inference|Module|Import|Manifest|Resolution|Diagnostic" -count=1`. **Done when:** semantic checker core has a success regression.
- [x] V020-0152. **Goal:** Add a negative semantic case for semantic checker core. **Files:** compiler/internal/semantics/checker.go, compiler/compiler_test.go. **Approach:** assert a positioned diagnostic for invalid assignment, call, import, manifest, or inference path. **Verification:** `go test ./compiler/... -run "Type|Inference|Module|Import|Manifest|Resolution|Diagnostic" -count=1`. **Done when:** semantic checker core has a failure regression.

## Epic 07 — Async, Tasks, Actors, Runtime ABI, And Selfhost Runtime

Stabilize local runtime features without pretending distributed runtime work is done.

- [x] V020-0301. **Goal:** Add parity coverage for async function MVP. **Files:** compiler/async_test.go, examples/async_smoke.tetra. **Approach:** compare builtin, selfhost, or target-specific behavior where the component owns parity. **Verification:** `go test ./compiler/... ./cli/... -run "Async|Await|Task|Actor|Actors|Runtime|Selfhost|ABI|Ownership|Stress" -count=1`. **Done when:** async function MVP cannot drift unnoticed.

## Epic 08 — IR, Lowering, Verification, And Unsupported Paths

Catch structural mistakes before they reach target-specific codegen.

- [x] V020-0351. **Goal:** Add verifier coverage for main lowering path. **Files:** compiler/internal/lower/lower.go, compiler/internal/lower/verify.go. **Approach:** assert structural invariants at the IR boundary. **Verification:** `go test ./compiler/internal/lower ./compiler -run "Lower|IR|Verify|Unsupported|Loop|Task|Actor|UI|Unsafe" -count=1`. **Done when:** main lowering path produces verifier-visible evidence.
- [x] V020-0352. **Goal:** Add unsupported-path diagnostics for main lowering path. **Files:** compiler/internal/lower/lower.go, compiler/internal/lower/verify.go. **Approach:** reject unsupported lowering with a clear diagnostic before backend codegen. **Verification:** `go test ./compiler/internal/lower ./compiler -run "Lower|IR|Verify|Unsupported|Loop|Task|Actor|UI|Unsafe" -count=1`. **Done when:** main lowering path fails before target-specific surprises.
- [x] V020-0353. **Goal:** Add target-neutral regression for main lowering path. **Files:** compiler/internal/lower/lower.go, compiler/internal/lower/verify.go. **Approach:** test lowering without depending on Linux/Windows/macOS output bytes when possible. **Verification:** `go test ./compiler/internal/lower ./compiler -run "Lower|IR|Verify|Unsupported|Loop|Task|Actor|UI|Unsafe" -count=1`. **Done when:** main lowering path is covered independently of object format.

## Epic 09 — Native x64 Backends, Linkers, Object Formats, And ABI

Keep Linux, Windows, and macOS native outputs buildable and schema-checked.

- [x] V020-0401. **Goal:** Add object-level assertion for shared x64 emitter. **Files:** compiler/internal/backend/x64/emitter.go, compiler/internal/backend/x64core/emit.go. **Approach:** inspect symbols, relocations, sections, or headers owned by this path. **Verification:** `go test ./compiler/internal/backend/... ./compiler/internal/linker/... ./compiler -run "ABI|ELF|PE|MachO|Object|Link|Runtime" -count=1`. **Done when:** shared x64 emitter has binary-structure coverage.
- [x] V020-0402. **Goal:** Add ABI edge case for shared x64 emitter. **Files:** compiler/internal/backend/x64/emitter.go, compiler/internal/backend/x64core/emit.go. **Approach:** cover stack args, register args, return values, or platform-specific call conventions. **Verification:** `go test ./compiler/internal/backend/... ./compiler/internal/linker/... ./compiler -run "ABI|ELF|PE|MachO|Object|Link|Runtime" -count=1`. **Done when:** shared x64 emitter has ABI regression coverage.

## Epic 10 — WASM, WASI, Web, UI Metadata, And Native Shell

Make build-only and UI-related targets easier to trust.

## Epic 11 — CLI Commands, JSON Reports, Exit Codes, And Help Text

Keep the command line stable and pleasant for real users.

## Epic 12 — LSP, API Docs, Generated Docs, And Editor Tooling

Raise editor and documentation tooling from useful alpha to repeatable v0.2.0 quality.

## Epic 15 — Examples, Smoke Matrix, Dogfood Projects, And User Proof

Make examples a reliable user-facing test suite rather than incidental files.

- [x] V020-0701. **Goal:** Add smoke-list coverage for basic language examples. **Files:** examples/hello.tetra, examples/flow_hello.tetra, examples/bool_smoke.tetra. **Approach:** ensure examples that should be release-covered appear in smoke list or documented exclusions. **Verification:** `./tetra fmt --check examples && ./tetra smoke --list --format=json | go run ./tools/cmd/validate-smoke-list && ./tetra test --report=json examples | go run ./tools/cmd/validate-test-report`. **Done when:** basic language examples has smoke matrix status.
- [x] V020-0702. **Goal:** Add expected-result evidence for basic language examples. **Files:** examples/hello.tetra, examples/flow_hello.tetra, examples/bool_smoke.tetra. **Approach:** record exit code, build-only behavior, or test report result. **Verification:** `./tetra fmt --check examples && ./tetra smoke --list --format=json | go run ./tools/cmd/validate-smoke-list && ./tetra test --report=json examples | go run ./tools/cmd/validate-test-report`. **Done when:** basic language examples has observable behavior.

## Epic 16 — Tool Validators, Test Wrappers, Generated Evidence, And Scripts

- [x] V020-0751. **Goal:** Add malformed fixture for test_all wrapper. **Files:** scripts/test_all.sh, tools/scriptstest/test_all_test.go. **Approach:** create a bad input that must fail with a clear message. **Verification:** `go test ./tools/... ./cli/... -count=1 && bash -n scripts/*.sh`. **Done when:** test_all wrapper rejects malformed data.

## Epic 17 — Performance, Caching, Reproducibility, And Binary Size

Improve speed and determinism only where it can be measured or guarded.

- [x] V020-0801. **Goal:** Add determinism assertion for compiler cache keys. **Files:** compiler/internal/cache/cache.go, compiler/internal/cache/cache_test.go, compiler/cache_test.go. **Approach:** compare stable hashes, ordered output, or repeatable report fields. **Verification:** `go test ./compiler/... ./tools/... -run "Cache|Turbo|Performance|Repro|Benchmark|Size|Determin" -count=1`. **Done when:** compiler cache keys is reproducible under identical inputs.
- [x] V020-0802. **Goal:** Add invalidation coverage for compiler cache keys. **Files:** compiler/internal/cache/cache.go, compiler/internal/cache/cache_test.go, compiler/cache_test.go. **Approach:** prove a relevant source, option, target, or dependency change is not incorrectly reused. **Verification:** `go test ./compiler/... ./tools/... -run "Cache|Turbo|Performance|Repro|Benchmark|Size|Determin" -count=1`. **Done when:** compiler cache keys invalidates stale data.

## Epic 18 — Security Review, Trust, Path Safety, And Artifact Integrity

Treat anything that writes files, runs tools, or packages artifacts as security-sensitive.

## Epic 19 — Documentation, Roadmaps, Historical Cleanup, And User Guides

Keep docs useful without letting old milestones lie about current release truth.

## Epic 20 — Final Verification Matrix And Release Closure

Define the concrete checks that close v0.2.0 only when evidence exists.

- [x] V020-0951. **Goal:** Make Go workspace tests a checklist item. **Files:** go.work, compiler/go.mod, cli/go.mod, tools/go.mod. **Approach:** add the exact command, output path, and expected pass condition to the v0.2.0 checklist. **Verification:** `go test ./compiler/... ./cli/... ./tools/... -count=1 && bash scripts/test_all.sh --quick && go run ./tools/cmd/verify-docs --manifest docs/generated/manifest.json && git diff --check`. **Done when:** Go workspace tests is visible in release planning.
- [x] V020-0952. **Goal:** Make Go workspace tests a gate step or explicit manual step. **Files:** go.work, compiler/go.mod, cli/go.mod, tools/go.mod. **Approach:** wire automation where possible and document manual signoff where required. **Verification:** `go test ./compiler/... ./cli/... ./tools/... -count=1 && bash scripts/test_all.sh --quick && go run ./tools/cmd/verify-docs --manifest docs/generated/manifest.json && git diff --check`. **Done when:** Go workspace tests cannot be forgotten.
- [x] V020-0953. **Goal:** Add failure triage for Go workspace tests. **Files:** go.work, compiler/go.mod, cli/go.mod, tools/go.mod. **Approach:** document how to interpret failure output and where logs are stored. **Verification:** `go test ./compiler/... ./cli/... ./tools/... -count=1 && bash scripts/test_all.sh --quick && go run ./tools/cmd/verify-docs --manifest docs/generated/manifest.json && git diff --check`. **Done when:** Go workspace tests failures are actionable.
